\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00287}00287\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Compute\ the\ distance\ matrix\ between\ each\ pair\ from\ a\ feature\ array\ X\ and\ Y.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00288}00288\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00289}00289\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ For\ efficiency\ reasons,\ the\ euclidean\ distance\ between\ a\ pair\ of\ row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00290}00290\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ vector\ x\ and\ y\ is\ computed\ as::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00291}00291\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00292}00292\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ dist(x,\ y)\ =\ sqrt(dot(x,\ x)\ -\/\ 2\ *\ dot(x,\ y)\ +\ dot(y,\ y))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00293}00293\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00294}00294\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ formulation\ has\ two\ advantages\ over\ other\ ways\ of\ computing\ distances.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00295}00295\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ First,\ it\ is\ computationally\ efficient\ when\ dealing\ with\ sparse\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00296}00296\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Second,\ if\ one\ argument\ varies\ but\ the\ other\ remains\ unchanged,\ then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00297}00297\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}dot(x,\ x)\`{}\ and/or\ \`{}dot(y,\ y)\`{}\ can\ be\ pre-\/computed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00298}00298\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00299}00299\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ However,\ this\ is\ not\ the\ most\ precise\ way\ of\ doing\ this\ computation,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00300}00300\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ because\ this\ equation\ potentially\ suffers\ from\ "{}catastrophic\ cancellation"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00301}00301\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Also,\ the\ distance\ matrix\ returned\ by\ this\ function\ may\ not\ be\ exactly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00302}00302\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ symmetric\ as\ required\ by,\ e.g.,\ :mod:\`{}scipy.spatial.distance\`{}\ functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00303}00303\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00613}00613\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ The\ increase\ amount\ of\ memory\ in\ 8-\/byte\ blocks\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00614}00614\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ -\/\ x\_density\ *\ batch\_size\ *\ n\_features\ (copy\ of\ chunk\ of\ X)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00617}00617\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ Hence\ x²\ +\ (xd+yd)kx\ =\ M,\ where\ x=batch\_size,\ k=n\_features,\ M=maxmem}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00618}00618\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xd=x\_density\ and\ yd=y\_density}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00619}00619\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ tmp\ =\ (x\_density\ +\ y\_density)\ *\ n\_features}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00620}00620\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ batch\_size\ =\ (-\/tmp\ +\ math.sqrt(tmp**2\ +\ 4\ *\ maxmem))\ /\ 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pairwise_8py_source_l00621}00621\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ batch\_size\ =\ max(int(batch\_size),\ 1)}
